< Text>
Awesome thrift store. You can catch some great deals on items here and personally I like finding those items that are not typically sold in stores anymore. Really good deals on items if you are looking to save money. Hours can kind of be confusing so I recommend calling in advance or getting the correct hours if you visit. They have certain hours for outside shopping and certain hours for inside, also special hours for their clients...< /Text>

Let's face it, threading is a not a pain-free experience, unless you are a robot.

First, sign in the front corner and wait.

My only qualm is that the waiting area is right next to the seat I was in.   The people sitting, waiting get a perpendicular view of what I'm getting done.   The angle allows no privacy at all.

She pointed out that my eyebrows aren't even.   But in the end, the result was fantastic!   I didn't notice how good of a job she did until I reached my car and inspected it in better lighting, the sun.   She made do with my "uneven eyebrows", they looked pretty congruent now.   I'm a happy camper.

Next time I'll check out their beauty supplies, looks like good stuff.< /text>

<Review>PLEASE READ BEFORE PURCHASING A VEHICLE

Wow what a disappointing experience with this dealership...It started off a little rocky to begin with. I saw a car on their lot on all the major websites (Autotrader, cars.com etc) for 18,999 which was admittedly a great deal for the car I was purchasing. I called ahead the day before and they seemed very accommodating and had the car ready for me to look at when I got there. During the test drive, three of the buttons for the infotainment system were stuck down like glue when I pushed them down. Figured no big deal, let the person showing me the car know and he assured me it would be fixed right away at no cost if i purchased the vehicle. I get to the pricing and it is 21,000 which was more than the price listed and when I looked it up to confirm the price the prices had increased in the 24 hours that I called ahead asking about the car. Luckily I had a picture of the original price and after a couple hours of them calling what must have been corporate they agreed to the offer which I thought was good. I made sure to get it in writing that would fix the buttons and the next day I brought it in is why this review is one star. Jason(the salesman) straight up asked for either the car back so they could sell it at its 21,000 price tag or that I would have to cover the buttons to be fixed out of my own pocket. When I brought up what was promised he mocked me by using semantics to say that promise letter was not legally binding and they would not fix the buttons on the car. I had to go back and forth with him for what had to have been an hour before he angrily stormed off when I would not give the car back to them after spending hours trying to buy it the day before, which was extremely rude and overtly unprofessional. Finally, after another 30 minutes of sitting and waiting, Nelson, the man who originally showed me the car and had originally promised the fix, came out and said that he talked to the manager and that he would take the heat so I could get the buttons fixed THAT THEY PROMISED TO FIX ORIGINALLY. He seemed like an excellent human being and was very apologetic. This was no doubt the worst and most anxiety inducing purchases I have made so far in my young life. the car itself is gorgeous and I absolutely love it, which is a shame that they ruined what otherwise would have been a super exciting purchase. PLEASE if you want to buy an Infiniti go to literally any other dealership theres one in Van Nuys and Valencia that would most likely stand behind their promises. If you HAVE to buy a car from them only ask to deal with Nelson as he was the only salesperson who treated me, the customer, with any respect at all. I hate writing bad reviews but I absolutely do not want anyone to have to go through the experience I did.</Review><Pictures>None< /Pictures>< resp>
